 Political Background: Jajpur Lok Sabha seat is reserved for Scheduled Castes
 is seat se abtak bijedy, congress or janata dal ke candidet chune gaye hai
 Congress's Ram Chandra Mallik won this seat in the 1962 Lok Sabha elections
 1967 main yahaan se piespi ke bi behera chunaav jite
 This seat came to Congress account in 1971
 1977 main ram chandra mallik bldi ke tikat par chunaav jite
 Anandi Charan Das won the Lok Sabha elections of 1980, 84, 89, 91 four times in a row
 1996 main janata dal ke anchal das ko jeet mili
 In 1998, Congress candidate Ram Chandra Mallik won the election
 1999 main is seat par bijedy ne entry kii or party candidet jagannatha malik ne chunaav jeeta
 After this, the Biju Janata Dal has been winning this seat for three consecutive times in 2004, 09 and 14
 2014 main party candidet reeta tarai ne sava teen lakh voton se jeet hasil kii
 Mythological significance of Jajpur The Jajpur region of Odisha is a place of historical and mythological importance
 yah vahi jagah he jahaan dharmik granthon main charchit baitarani nadi bahati he

 This place is nowadays known as 'jajpur'
 jajpur jile main kai puranic mandir hai jo sthapatth kala kaa beshkeemtee namoona hai

 Marumalarachi Dravida Munnetra Kazhagam (MDMK), the party of the fiercest Tamil leader Vaiko, said in its manifesto issued on Saturday that it would change the name of the country to 'united States of India' if it had to play a part in forming the government after the Lok Sabha elections
 party ne yah bhi kaha he ki vah libration tigers of tamil ilam (littey) par se pratibandh khatm kar degi
 According to MDMK, at the time the Indian Constitution was written, it was promised to create a framework of federal governance
 party ne kaha he ki jin logon ne shuru main 'anekta main ekta' kaa daawa kiya tha, baad main ve dhire-dhire centre sarkaar ko shakti kaa centre banane main jute gaye
 The party has said that to strengthen the unity of the country, the Indian Constitution should be reconsidered and the country should be named 'united States of India' on the lines of the United States of America
 party ne kaha he ki vah iske liye ladaai ladegi
 The party has demanded the central government to transfer the rights related to education to the state and said that the basic powers mentioned in the constitution should be fully given to the states
 party ne kaha he ki vah srilanka main srilankai tamilon ke liye ilam gathit kiye jane par janamat sangrah karaayegi
 According to MDMK, a referendum should be held in the areas where Sri Lankan Tamils live
 party ne jin deshon main tamilon kii acchhee khaasi aabaadi nivas karti he, vahaan tamil rajdoot niyukt karne or mrityudand par pratibandh lagane kaa vaada kiya he

 2009 ke loksabhaa chunaav main bhi aisa hi sameekaran ulajhaa tha

 unhen 1,82,789 vot mili

 patil ko 1,41,425 vot mili

 According to the findings published in the journal Nature Medicine, the research team at Louvain University conducted studies on effective bacteria in the human body
 iske liye 42 pratibhaagiyon ko namankit kiya gaya or 32 ne is pareekshan ko puraa kiya
 Researchers gave akaramensia to obese participants, all with diabetes type 2 and metabolic syndrome
 yani inamen dil kii bimariyon se sambandhit jokhim kaarak the
 The participants were divided into three groups — one who took live bacteria and two who ingested pasteurized bacteria — the members of both groups were asked to change their food and physical activity
 inhen akkarmensia neutrishnal supplement ke taur par diya gaya
 These participants were to be consumed for three months continuously
 shodhakartaaon ne paaya ki is supplement ko khaanaa aasaan rahaa or jivit or paschurikrut bacteria lene vaale samoohon main koi said effect nahin dekha gaya
 Pasteurized bacteria significantly reduced the risk of diabetes 2 and heart diseases in participants
 isse liver ke swasthya main bhi sudhaar dekha gaya, pratibhaagiyon ke shaareerik vajan main bhi giravat (saamanyataur par 2
 3 kg) were observed and at the same time a decrease in cholesterol levels
